Envoy is organized into a layered architecture with both legacy and unified implementations:\\n\\n## Core Architecture\\n\\n### 1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl (Adapter Pattern)\\nThe primary entry point is `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc`. This class acts as an adapter from typed Subscription to untyped GrpcMux, handling per-xDS API statistics and logging. It manages the lifecycle of xDS subscriptions and interfaces with the underlying mux implementations.\\n\\n### 2. Factory Selection (SotW vs Delta)\\nThe `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory`, `DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory`, and `AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory` classes in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc` are responsible for creating the appropriate mux implementation. The factory checks the runtime feature flag `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux` to decide between:\\n\\n- **Unified XdsMux implementations**: Uses `GrpcMuxSotw` or `GrpcMuxDelta` from the new XdsMux namespace\\n- **Legacy implementations**: Falls back to `GrpcMuxImpl` (SotW) or `NewGrpcMuxImpl` (Delta)\\n\\n### 3. Unified XdsMux Template Architecture\\nThe file `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc` contains a unified template-based implementation:\\n\\n**Template Class**: `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` where:\\n- `S` = SubscriptionState type (either `SotwSubscriptionState` or `DeltaSubscriptionState`)\\n- `F` = SubscriptionStateFactory type\\n- `RQ` = Request protobuf type\\n- `RS` = Response protobuf type\\n\\nThis template is instantiated as:\\n- `GrpcMuxSotw` - For SotW protocol using `DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse`\\n- `GrpcMuxDelta` - For Delta protocol using `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`/`DeltaDiscoveryResponse`\\n\\n### 4. State of the World (SotW) Implementation\\nThe `SotwSubscriptionState` class in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc` implements the SotW protocol logic. It tracks version information and nonces for complete resource responses. The `SotwSubscriptionStateFactory` creates instances of this state.\\n\\n### 5. Delta xDS Implementation\\nThe `DeltaSubscriptionState` class in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc` implements the Delta protocol logic. It tracks per-resource versions and handles incremental resource updates. The `DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory` creates instances.\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**GrpcStream Management**:\\n- `grpc_stream_interface.h`: Abstract interface for gRPC streams\\n- `grpc_stream.h`: Template implementation of gRPC stream\\n- `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Multiplexes between primary and failover xDS sources\\n\\n**Resource Management**:\\n- `watch_map.h/cc`: Maps watches to resources and delivers updates\\n- `update_ack.h`: Tracks ACKs for xDS responses\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.h/cc`: Manages ACKs with pause/resume semantics\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.h/cc`: Caches EDS (Endpoint Discovery Service) resources\\n\\n**Subscription Management**:\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h`: Configuration context for mux creation\\n- `xds_source_id.h/cc`: Source identification for xDS\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc`: Factory for resource collection subscriptions\\n\\n### 7. Legacy Implementations\\nFor backward compatibility, the codebase retains:\\n- `GrpcMuxImpl` (in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`) - Original SotW implementation\\n- `NewGrpcMuxImpl` (in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`) - Original Delta implementation\\n- `DeltaSubscriptionState` (in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`) - Legacy Delta state\\n\\n## Protocol Flow\\n\\n1. GrpcSubscriptionImpl (Adapter Pattern)\\nThe primary entry point is `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc`.
